# 自动分配军用工厂生产陆装/空军装备（仿原版 AI 三层需求模型）。on_monthly 对玩家调用。
# 与海军生产（auto_production_naval，逐日调用）拆分为独立文件：陆/空装备产能变化慢，按月重算即可；
# 海军 amount=1 自闭合线产完即空闲，需按天检查以尽快重开新线。
# 第1+2层 缺口+储备：缺口 = (部队需求-在用) + 0.8x在用 - 库存（部队满编后仍补库存到在用量 80% 作战损储备，
#   仿原版 PRODUCTION_EQUIPMENT_SURPLUS_FACTOR=0.8）；飞机目标库存 = max(100, 0.8x在役架数)。
# 第3层 盈余：前两层分完仍有空闲军工 -> 按权重分给全部品类（无论是否在用，未在用装备也囤货）
#   （步兵1 支援1 火炮1 战斗机1 自火10 坦歼5），库存上限 = max(2x在用,100)，超上限退出；
#   全部到顶则无视上限继续按权重分给全部品类——工厂永不闲置。
# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口x单件造价/400)（400≈单厂3个月IC产出）；两阶段：先算全部分配，再每类至多开一条线。
# 防刷线（无冷却）：永久线标记 autocore_line_<key>；首开保底1厂（允许超池，防缺装提示），
#   重复开线直接保底5厂（池耗尽则不开，攒出空闲军工的当天一次开够）。
# 空闲 >= 90% 总军工（视为手动清空队列）-> 清除全部线标记，本 tick 按首开逻辑重新分配。
# 步枪线最先创建（队列最顶、优先分厂）且确有缺口时按至少 10000 把计。
# 开线型号 = 已研最新科技；MIO 逐级择优（专业 trait / 装备类型识别），无匹配则裸线。
# 由脚本自动生成，勿手改。
auto_production = {
	# ===== 军工分配 =====
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { num_of_available_military_factories > 0.5 } }
		# 清空队列检测：空闲 >= 90% 总军工 -> 清除全部线标记，恢复首开保底逻辑
		set_variable = { prod_total = num_of_military_factories }
		multiply_variable = { prod_total = 0.9 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { num_of_available_military_factories > prod_total } }
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_infantry
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_support
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_antitank
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_antiair
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_artillery
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_mechanized
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_motorized
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_flame
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_td
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_spg
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_cas
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_fighter
			clr_country_flag = autocore_line_cvcas
		}
		set_variable = { prod_left = num_of_available_military_factories }
		# ===== 阶段1：计算各类分配（只算不开） =====
		# --- 步兵装备（单件造价 0.5） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
					has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
					has_tech = infantry_weapons1
					has_tech = infantry_weapons
				}
			}
			# 缺口 = (需求 - 在用) + 0.8 x 在用 - 库存（战损储备缓冲，仿原版 0.8 系数）
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
			set_variable = { prod_buf = num_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { prod_buf = 0.2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = prod_buf }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@infantry_equipment }
			# 前期步枪需求增长快于缺口结算：确有缺口时按至少 10000 把计（无缺口不触发，防无限刷线）
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0 }
					check_variable = { prod_deficit < 10000 }
				}
				set_variable = { prod_deficit = 10000 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0.5 } }
				# 保底：首开 1 厂，重复开线 5 厂
				set_variable = { prod_min = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_infantry } }
					set_variable = { prod_min = 1 }
				}
				# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 x 单件造价 0.5 ÷ 400)
				set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
				multiply_variable = { prod_want = 0.5 }
				divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
				add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
				round_variable = prod_want
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < prod_min } }
					set_variable = { prod_want = prod_min }
				}
				# 重复线需池中尚有空闲才开（防逐日刷线）；首开线永远开
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_infantry }
						}
					}
					# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，再抬到保底（允许略超池）
					set_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = prod_want }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry > prod_left } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = prod_left }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry < prod_min } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = prod_min }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_infantry }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 支援装备（单件造价 4） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_support = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@support_equipment > 0 }
				has_tech = tech_support
			}
			# 缺口 = (需求 - 在用) + 0.8 x 在用 - 库存（战损储备缓冲，仿原版 0.8 系数）
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@support_equipment }
			set_variable = { prod_buf = num_equipment_in_armies@support_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { prod_buf = 0.2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = prod_buf }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@support_equipment }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0.5 } }
				# 保底：首开 1 厂，重复开线 5 厂
				set_variable = { prod_min = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_support } }
					set_variable = { prod_min = 1 }
				}
				# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 x 单件造价 4 ÷ 400)
				set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
				multiply_variable = { prod_want = 4 }
				divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
				add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
				round_variable = prod_want
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < prod_min } }
					set_variable = { prod_want = prod_min }
				}
				# 重复线需池中尚有空闲才开（防逐日刷线）；首开线永远开
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_support }
						}
					}
					# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，再抬到保底（允许略超池）
					set_variable = { prod_alloc_support = prod_want }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_support > prod_left } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_support = prod_left }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_support < prod_min } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_support = prod_min }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_support }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 反坦克炮（单件造价 4） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@anti_tank_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					has_tech = antitank5
					has_tech = antitank2
					has_tech = interwar_antitank
				}
			}
			# 缺口 = (需求 - 在用) + 0.8 x 在用 - 库存（战损储备缓冲，仿原版 0.8 系数）
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@anti_tank_equipment }
			set_variable = { prod_buf = num_equipment_in_armies@anti_tank_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { prod_buf = 0.2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = prod_buf }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@anti_tank_equipment }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0.5 } }
				# 保底：首开 1 厂，重复开线 5 厂
				set_variable = { prod_min = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_antitank } }
					set_variable = { prod_min = 1 }
				}
				# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 x 单件造价 4 ÷ 400)
				set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
				multiply_variable = { prod_want = 4 }
				divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
				add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
				round_variable = prod_want
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < prod_min } }
					set_variable = { prod_want = prod_min }
				}
				# 重复线需池中尚有空闲才开（防逐日刷线）；首开线永远开
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_antitank }
						}
					}
					# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，再抬到保底（允许略超池）
					set_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = prod_want }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank > prod_left } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = prod_left }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank < prod_min } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_antitank = prod_min }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_antitank }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 防空炮（单件造价 4） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@anti_air_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					has_tech = antiair5
					has_tech = antiair2
					has_tech = interwar_antiair
				}
			}
			# 缺口 = (需求 - 在用) + 0.8 x 在用 - 库存（战损储备缓冲，仿原版 0.8 系数）
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@anti_air_equipment }
			set_variable = { prod_buf = num_equipment_in_armies@anti_air_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { prod_buf = 0.2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = prod_buf }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@anti_air_equipment }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0.5 } }
				# 保底：首开 1 厂，重复开线 5 厂
				set_variable = { prod_min = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_antiair } }
					set_variable = { prod_min = 1 }
				}
				# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 x 单件造价 4 ÷ 400)
				set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
				multiply_variable = { prod_want = 4 }
				divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
				add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
				round_variable = prod_want
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < prod_min } }
					set_variable = { prod_want = prod_min }
				}
				# 重复线需池中尚有空闲才开（防逐日刷线）；首开线永远开
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_antiair }
						}
					}
					# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，再抬到保底（允许略超池）
					set_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = prod_want }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair > prod_left } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = prod_left }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair < prod_min } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_antiair = prod_min }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_antiair }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 火炮（单件造价 3.5） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@artillery_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					has_tech = artillery4
					has_tech = artillery1
					has_tech = gw_artillery
				}
			}
			# 缺口 = (需求 - 在用) + 0.8 x 在用 - 库存（战损储备缓冲，仿原版 0.8 系数）
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@artillery_equipment }
			set_variable = { prod_buf = num_equipment_in_armies@artillery_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { prod_buf = 0.2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = prod_buf }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@artillery_equipment }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0.5 } }
				# 保底：首开 1 厂，重复开线 5 厂
				set_variable = { prod_min = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_artillery } }
					set_variable = { prod_min = 1 }
				}
				# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 x 单件造价 3.5 ÷ 400)
				set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
				multiply_variable = { prod_want = 3.5 }
				divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
				add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
				round_variable = prod_want
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < prod_min } }
					set_variable = { prod_want = prod_min }
				}
				# 重复线需池中尚有空闲才开（防逐日刷线）；首开线永远开
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_artillery }
						}
					}
					# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，再抬到保底（允许略超池）
					set_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = prod_want }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery > prod_left } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = prod_left }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery < prod_min } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = prod_min }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_artillery }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 机械化（单件造价 8） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@mechanized_equipment > 0 }
				OR = {
					has_tech = mechanised_infantry3
					has_tech = mechanised_infantry2
					has_tech = mechanised_infantry
				}
			}
			# 缺口 = (需求 - 在用) + 0.8 x 在用 - 库存（战损储备缓冲，仿原版 0.8 系数）
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@mechanized_equipment }
			set_variable = { prod_buf = num_equipment_in_armies@mechanized_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { prod_buf = 0.2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = prod_buf }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@mechanized_equipment }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0.5 } }
				# 保底：首开 1 厂，重复开线 5 厂
				set_variable = { prod_min = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_mechanized } }
					set_variable = { prod_min = 1 }
				}
				# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 x 单件造价 8 ÷ 400)
				set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
				multiply_variable = { prod_want = 8 }
				divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
				add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
				round_variable = prod_want
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < prod_min } }
					set_variable = { prod_want = prod_min }
				}
				# 重复线需池中尚有空闲才开（防逐日刷线）；首开线永远开
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_mechanized }
						}
					}
					# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，再抬到保底（允许略超池）
					set_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = prod_want }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized > prod_left } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = prod_left }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized < prod_min } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_mechanized = prod_min }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_mechanized }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 摩托化（单件造价 2.5） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@motorized_equipment > 0 }
				has_tech = motorised_infantry
			}
			# 缺口 = (需求 - 在用) + 0.8 x 在用 - 库存（战损储备缓冲，仿原版 0.8 系数）
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@motorized_equipment }
			set_variable = { prod_buf = num_equipment_in_armies@motorized_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { prod_buf = 0.2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = prod_buf }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@motorized_equipment }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0.5 } }
				# 保底：首开 1 厂，重复开线 5 厂
				set_variable = { prod_min = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_motorized } }
					set_variable = { prod_min = 1 }
				}
				# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 x 单件造价 2.5 ÷ 400)
				set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
				multiply_variable = { prod_want = 2.5 }
				divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
				add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
				round_variable = prod_want
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < prod_min } }
					set_variable = { prod_want = prod_min }
				}
				# 重复线需池中尚有空闲才开（防逐日刷线）；首开线永远开
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_motorized }
						}
					}
					# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，再抬到保底（允许略超池）
					set_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = prod_want }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized > prod_left } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = prod_left }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized < prod_min } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_motorized = prod_min }
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = prod_alloc_motorized }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# --- 喷火坦克（单件造价 4） ---
		set_variable = { prod_alloc_flame = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { num_target_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_flame_chassis > 0 }
			}
			# 缺口 = (需求 - 在用) + 0.8 x 在用 - 库存（战损储备缓冲，仿原版 0.8 系数）
			set_variable = { prod_deficit = num_target_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_flame_chassis }
			set_variable = { prod_buf = num_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_flame_chassis }
			multiply_variable = { prod_buf = 0.2 }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = prod_buf }
			subtract_from_variable = { prod_deficit = num_equipment@medium_tank_flame_chassis }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { prod_deficit > 0.5 } }
				# 保底：首开 1 厂，重复开线 5 厂
				set_variable = { prod_min = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_flame } }
					set_variable = { prod_min = 1 }
				}
				# 需求厂数 = ceil(缺口 x 单件造价 4 ÷ 400)
				set_variable = { prod_want = prod_deficit }
				multiply_variable = { prod_want = 4 }
				divide_variable = { prod_want = 400 }
				add_to_variable = { prod_want = 0.49 }
				round_variable = prod_want
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_want < prod_min } }
					set_variable = { prod_want = prod_min }
				}
				# 重复线需池中尚有空闲才开（防逐日刷线）；首开线永远开
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
							NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_line_flame }
						}
					}
					# 分配 = min(需求, 剩余空闲)，再抬到保底（允许略超池）
					set_variable = { prod_alloc_flame = prod_want }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_flame > prod_left } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_flame = prod_left }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_alloc_flame < prod_min } }
						set_variable = { prod_alloc_flame = prod_min }
					}

						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }

				}
			}
		}
		# ===== 盈余分配：需求全满足后按权重分掉剩余空闲军工 =====
		# 不论是否在用，全部品类参与（未在用的也囤货）；库存上限 = max(2x在用,100) 的类退出；份额保底 5 厂
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 } }
			set_variable = { srp_sum = 0 }
			# 步兵装备（权重 1）
			set_variable = { srp_w_infantry = 0 }
			set_variable = { srp_cap = num_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { srp_cap = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { srp_cap < 100 } }
				set_variable = { srp_cap = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { num_equipment@infantry_equipment < srp_cap }
				}
				set_variable = { srp_w_infantry = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 1 }
			}
			# 支援装备（权重 1）
			set_variable = { srp_w_support = 0 }
			set_variable = { srp_cap = num_equipment_in_armies@support_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { srp_cap = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { srp_cap < 100 } }
				set_variable = { srp_cap = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { num_equipment@support_equipment < srp_cap }
				}
				set_variable = { srp_w_support = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 1 }
			}
			# 火炮（权重 1）
			set_variable = { srp_w_artillery = 0 }
			set_variable = { srp_cap = num_equipment_in_armies@artillery_equipment }
			multiply_variable = { srp_cap = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { srp_cap < 100 } }
				set_variable = { srp_cap = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { num_equipment@artillery_equipment < srp_cap }
				}
				set_variable = { srp_w_artillery = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 1 }
			}
			# 战斗机（权重 1）
			set_variable = { srp_w_fighter = 0 }
			set_variable = { srp_cap = num_deployed_planes_with_type@fighter }
			multiply_variable = { srp_cap = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { srp_cap < 100 } }
				set_variable = { srp_cap = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { num_equipment@small_plane_airframe < srp_cap }
				}
				set_variable = { srp_w_fighter = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 1 }
			}
			# 自行火炮（权重 10）
			set_variable = { srp_w_spg = 0 }
			set_variable = { srp_cap = num_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_artillery_chassis }
			multiply_variable = { srp_cap = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { srp_cap < 100 } }
				set_variable = { srp_cap = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { num_equipment@medium_tank_artillery_chassis < srp_cap }
				}
				set_variable = { srp_w_spg = 10 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 10 }
			}
			# 坦克歼击车（权重 5）
			set_variable = { srp_w_td = 0 }
			set_variable = { srp_cap = num_equipment_in_armies@medium_tank_destroyer_chassis }
			multiply_variable = { srp_cap = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { srp_cap < 100 } }
				set_variable = { srp_cap = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { num_equipment@medium_tank_destroyer_chassis < srp_cap }
				}
				set_variable = { srp_w_td = 5 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 5 }
			}
			# 全部到顶：无视库存上限，仍按权重分给全部品类（工厂永不闲置）
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { srp_sum < 0.5 } }
				set_variable = { srp_w_infantry = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 1 }
				set_variable = { srp_w_support = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 1 }
				set_variable = { srp_w_artillery = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 1 }
				set_variable = { srp_w_fighter = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 1 }
				set_variable = { srp_w_spg = 10 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 10 }
				set_variable = { srp_w_td = 5 }
				add_to_variable = { srp_sum = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { srp_sum > 0.5 } }
				set_variable = { srp_base = prod_left }
				# 步兵装备：份额 = 剩余 x 权重 ÷ 权重和，保底 5 厂
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { srp_w_infantry > 0.5 }
						check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
					}
					set_variable = { srp_share = srp_base }
					multiply_variable = { srp_share = srp_w_infantry }
					divide_variable = { srp_share = srp_sum }
					round_variable = srp_share
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_share < 5 } }
						set_variable = { srp_share = 5 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = srp_share }
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = srp_share }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
				# 支援装备：份额 = 剩余 x 权重 ÷ 权重和，保底 5 厂
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { srp_w_support > 0.5 }
						check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
					}
					set_variable = { srp_share = srp_base }
					multiply_variable = { srp_share = srp_w_support }
					divide_variable = { srp_share = srp_sum }
					round_variable = srp_share
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_share < 5 } }
						set_variable = { srp_share = 5 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_support = srp_share }
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = srp_share }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
				# 火炮：份额 = 剩余 x 权重 ÷ 权重和，保底 5 厂
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { srp_w_artillery > 0.5 }
						check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
					}
					set_variable = { srp_share = srp_base }
					multiply_variable = { srp_share = srp_w_artillery }
					divide_variable = { srp_share = srp_sum }
					round_variable = srp_share
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_share < 5 } }
						set_variable = { srp_share = 5 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = srp_share }
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = srp_share }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
				# 战斗机：份额 = 剩余 x 权重 ÷ 权重和，保底 5 厂
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { srp_w_fighter > 0.5 }
						check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
					}
					set_variable = { srp_share = srp_base }
					multiply_variable = { srp_share = srp_w_fighter }
					divide_variable = { srp_share = srp_sum }
					round_variable = srp_share
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_share < 5 } }
						set_variable = { srp_share = 5 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter = srp_share }
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = srp_share }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
				# 自行火炮：份额 = 剩余 x 权重 ÷ 权重和，保底 5 厂
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { srp_w_spg > 0.5 }
						check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
					}
					set_variable = { srp_share = srp_base }
					multiply_variable = { srp_share = srp_w_spg }
					divide_variable = { srp_share = srp_sum }
					round_variable = srp_share
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_share < 5 } }
						set_variable = { srp_share = 5 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_spg = srp_share }
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = srp_share }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
				# 坦克歼击车：份额 = 剩余 x 权重 ÷ 权重和，保底 5 厂
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { srp_w_td > 0.5 }
						check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 }
					}
					set_variable = { srp_share = srp_base }
					multiply_variable = { srp_share = srp_w_td }
					divide_variable = { srp_share = srp_sum }
					round_variable = srp_share
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_share < 5 } }
						set_variable = { srp_share = 5 }
					}
					add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_td = srp_share }
					subtract_from_variable = { prod_left = srp_share }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { prod_left < 0 } }
						set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
					}
				}
				# 取整残留 -> 给权重最高的参与类
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { prod_left > 0.5 } }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_w_infantry > 0.5 } }
						add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_infantry = prod_left }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_w_support > 0.5 } }
						add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_support = prod_left }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_w_artillery > 0.5 } }
						add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_artillery = prod_left }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_w_fighter > 0.5 } }
						add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_fighter = prod_left }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_w_spg > 0.5 } }
						add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_spg = prod_left }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { srp_w_td > 0.5 } }
						add_to_variable = { prod_alloc_td = prod_left }
					}
					set_variable = { prod_left = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
